The cake made the cat's toe feel better and Jane and her brother were filled with joy.

Original Story: Once upon a time there was a spider named Sunny. One day, Sunny was so excited for a picnic that he loaded his picnic basket with all sorts of wonderful treats. As Sunny began to walk away a sweet butterfly flew by and asked him what he was doing. "I'm going to a picnic!" Sunny chirped with excitement. "That sounds lovely," the butterfly said. "Can I join you?"Sunny was more than happy to share his picnic with the butterfly. As Sunny continued to load his basket, the butterfly flew ahead to meet his friends at the picnic. When Sunny arrived, he was surprised to see that the butterfly had already put out his own picnic blanket and invited all the animals to join.Sunny and his friends feasted on the sweets he had brought with him while they all laughed and talked. They all had such a wonderful time, and Sunny realized that sharing is sweeter than eating alone. From then on, Sunny always liked to load his picnic basket with extra treats to share with his friends whenever he went on adventures. The moral of the story is that sharing is sweet and it is so much fun to share an adventure with friends.
Original Summary: Sunny the spider learns that sharing is sweeter than eating alone when he invites a butterfly to join him on a picnic and shares his treats with his friends, leading him to always load his picnic basket with extra treats to share with others on his adventures.

Original Story: Once upon a time a small grey mouse was scurrying around in a dry field. All of a sudden it heard something far away and it quickly wanted to hide. He gazed around the tree and slowly stepped closer to the small grey mouse.The mouse stayed very still, not wanting to move a muscle. The owl slowly looked around before he turned away and flew away. When the owl was gone, the mouse let out a huge breath and looked around. The field was quiet and the mouse knew he was safe.The mouse scurried off the tree and ran into a small hole. Inside the hole it was warm and cozy. The mouse curled up and fell asleep. Outside all was quiet and dry and the mouse stayed safe and snug in its little home.

Original Story: Tom is a turtle. He has a big family. He has a mom, a dad, and four brothers. They live in a pond with many other turtles. Tom likes his family, but he also likes to move. He swims closer to the truck. He sees a man with a net. The man is catching turtles and putting them in a box."Hey, stop!" Tom shouts. "What are you doing?"The man does not hear Tom. He sees Tom and tries to catch him too. Tom is scared. He swims away. He looks for his family. He sees them in the corner of the pond. They are hiding under some plants."Tom, come here!" his mom calls. "It's not safe!"Tom swims to his mom. He hugs her. He is glad to see her. He tells her what he saw."That's a bad man," his dad says. They catch the man's attention."Wow, look at those turtles!" the man says. "They are so colorful. They are so unique. I have to catch them all. They will make me rich."The man drops the box. He grabs the net. He runs to the pond. He tries to catch the turtles. But the turtles are faster. They swim away. They swim around the man. They confuse him. They make him dizzy. They make him fall. He drops the net. He drops his hat. He drops his keys.The turtles see the keys. They see the box. They see the other turtles. They swim to the box. They use the keys to open the box. They free the other turtles. They tell them to run. They tell them to hide. They tell them to be careful.The other turtles thank them. They are happy. They are grateful. They are free.The man gets up. He is angry. He is wet. He is muddy. He looks for the turtles. He looks for the box. He looks for the keys. He sees nothing. He hears nothing. He is too late.The turtles are gone. They are safe. They are back in the pond. They are with their family. They are unique. They are proud. They are happy. They are turtles.
